    <td style="font-size: 10pt"><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; font-size: 10pt"><b>Departure of Directors or Certain Officers; Election of Directors; Appointment of Certain Officers; Compensatory Arrangement of Certain Officers.</b></span></td></tr>

<p style="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">On February&#160;13, 2025, the Board of Directors
(the &#8220;Board&#8221;) of AbbVie Inc. (the &#8220;Company&#8221;) unanimously elected Robert A. Michael to succeed Richard A. Gonzalez
as the Company&#8217;s Chairman, effective July&#160;1, 2025. Mr.&#160;Gonzalez, who has served as Chairman since the Company&#8217;s
formation in 2013, will retire from the Board, effective July&#160;1, 2025. Mr.&#160;Michael is the Company&#8217;s current Chief Executive
Officer, as well as a director on the Board.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><span style="font-size: 10pt">On February&#160;13,
2025, Glenn F. Tilton informed the Company of his decision to retire as a director, effective July&#160;1, 2025</span><span style="background-color: white">.</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" style="width: 100%; border-collapse: collapse; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif">
  <tr style="vertical-align: top">
    <td style="width: 11%; font-size: 10pt"><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; font-size: 10pt"><b>Item 7.01</b></span></td>
    <td style="font-size: 10pt"><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; font-size: 10pt"><b>Regulation FD Disclosure.</b></span></td></tr>
  </table>
<p style="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">On February&#160;14, 2025, the Company issued a
press release announcing the appointment of Mr.&#160;Michael as Chairman, effective July&#160;1, 2025. A copy of the press release is
furnished as Exhibit&#160;99.1 to this Current Report on Form&#160;8-K.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><span style="font-size: 10pt">The information in
this Item 7.01, including Exhibit&#160;99.1 attached hereto, is being furnished and shall not be deemed &#8220;filed&#8221; for the purposes
of Section&#160;18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended (the &#8220;Exchange Act&#8221;), or otherwise subject to the liabilities
of that Section&#160;and shall not be incorporated by reference into any registration statement or other document filed pursuant to the
Securities Act of 1933, as amended, or the Exchange Act, except as otherwise expressly stated in such filing</span><span style="background-color: white">.</span></p>

<DESCRIPTION>EXHIBIT 99.1
<TEXT>
<HTML>
<HEAD>
     <TITLE></TITLE>
</HEAD>
<BODY STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">

<P STYLE="margin: 0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: right; margin: 0pt"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; font-size: 11pt"><B>Exhibit 99.1</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="margin: 0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 16pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; color: #071d49"><B>PRESS RELEASE</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 14pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><B>AbbVie Appoints CEO Robert A. Michael as Chairman of the Board of
Directors</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 11pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in">-</TD><TD><I>Richard A. Gonzalez to retire from the board of directors effective July&nbsp;1, 2025</I></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><B>NORTH CHICAGO,&nbsp;Ill., February&nbsp;14, 2025</B> -- AbbVie (NYSE:
ABBV) today announced that its board of directors has unanimously elected chief executive officer (CEO) Robert A. Michael to assume the
additional position of chairman, effective July&nbsp;1, 2025. He will succeed&nbsp;Richard A. Gonzalez, who formerly served as AbbVie&rsquo;s
CEO and has been chairman since the Company&rsquo;s formation in 2013.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&quot;I want to extend my heartfelt gratitude to Rick for his remarkable
leadership and dedicated service,&quot; said Roxanne S. Austin, lead independent director. &quot;The board and I have complete confidence
in Rob, and we are fortunate to have him assume the role of chairman. Rob is a visionary leader who operates with integrity and a steadfast
commitment to AbbVie, its people, patients and shareholders. He is the right leader to guide this company into its next phase of growth.&quot;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&ldquo;I am honored to take on the role of chairman,&rdquo; said Robert
A. Michael, chief executive officer. &ldquo;On behalf of our employees around the world,&nbsp;I extend my sincere gratitude to Rick for
his exceptional leadership over the past 12 years. I look forward to partnering with the board to build on AbbVie&rsquo;s track record
of success and to make a remarkable impact for our patients, employees, shareholders and communities.&rdquo;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&quot;I am deeply grateful to the board for their strategic vision and
support over the past 12 years,&quot; said Richard A. Gonzalez, executive chairman of the board and former chief executive officer. &quot;Serving
alongside the talented people of AbbVie has been the greatest privilege of my career. I am confident that Rob and the board will successfully
lead AbbVie into the future, continuing to deliver groundbreaking medicines for our patients and creating tremendous value for our shareholders.&quot;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0">In addition, Glenn F. Tilton will retire from AbbVie&rsquo;s board effective
July&nbsp;1, 2025. Mr.&nbsp;Tilton served as lead independent director from 2013 to 2024 and was succeeded by Ms.&nbsp;Austin in July&nbsp;2024.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><B>About Robert A. Michael</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0">Mr.&nbsp;Michael is AbbVie&rsquo;s chief executive officer (CEO). Prior
to being named CEO, Mr.&nbsp;Michael was president and chief operating officer of AbbVie and has been a longstanding member of the Company&rsquo;s
Executive Leadership Team. From establishing AbbVie&rsquo;s first financial planning organization, to developing its diversified business
strategy, to successfully navigating the end of exclusivity for Humira in the U.S., Mr.&nbsp;Michael has been integral to AbbVie's success
and growth over the years. In the role of president and chief operating officer, Mr.&nbsp;Michael was responsible for global commercial
operations, finance, corporate human resources, global operations, business development and corporate strategy for the company. He was
previously appointed vice chairman and president in 2022, vice chairman, finance and commercial operations in 2021 and chief financial
officer in 2018. Mr.&nbsp;Michael has more than 32 years of</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0"></P>

<!-- Field: Page; Sequence: 1 -->
    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 12pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid"><P STYLE="margin: 0pt">&nbsp;</P></DIV>
    <DIV STYLE="break-before: page; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 12pt"><P STYLE="margin: 0pt">&nbsp;</P></DIV>
    <!-- Field: /Page -->

<P STYLE="font: 11pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0">experience including leadership roles across multiple businesses, including
pharmaceuticals, aesthetics, diagnostics, diabetes care and nutrition. He began his career with Abbott as a member of the financial development
program.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><B>About AbbVie</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0">AbbVie's mission is to discover and deliver innovative medicines and
solutions that solve serious health issues today and address the medical challenges of tomorrow. We strive to have a remarkable impact
on people's lives across several key therapeutic areas &ndash; immunology, oncology, neuroscience, and eye care &ndash; and products
and services in our Allergan Aesthetics portfolio. For more information about AbbVie, please visit us at&nbsp;<U>www.abbvie.com</U>.
Follow @abbvie on&nbsp;<U>LinkedIn,</U>&nbsp;<U>Facebook</U>,&nbsp;<U>Instagram</U>,&nbsp;<U>X (formerly Twitter)</U>, and&nbsp;<U>YouTube</U>.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><B>AbbVie Forward-Looking Statements</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><I>Some statements in this news release are, or may be considered, forward-looking
statements for purposes of the Private Securities Litigation Reform Act of 1995. The words &quot;believe,&quot; &quot;expect,&quot; &quot;anticipate,&quot;
&quot;project&quot; and similar expressions and uses of future or conditional verbs, generally identify forward-looking statements. AbbVie
cautions that these forward-looking statements are subject to risks and uncertainties that may cause actual results to differ materially
from those expressed or implied in the forward-looking statements. Such risks and uncertainties include, but are not limited to, challenges
to intellectual property, competition from other products, difficulties inherent in the research and development process, adverse litigation
or government action, and changes to laws and regulations applicable to our industry. Additional information about the economic, competitive,
governmental, technological and other factors that may affect AbbVie's operations is set forth in Item 1A, &quot;Risk Factors,&quot; of
AbbVie's 2023 Annual Report on Form&nbsp;10-K, which has been filed with the Securities and Exchange Commission, as updated by its subsequent
Quarterly Reports on Form&nbsp;10-Q. AbbVie undertakes no obligation, and specifically declines, to release publicly any revisions to
forward-looking statements as a result of subsequent events or developments, except as required by law.</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>
